}}</h2>\n            <p>Author: {{ book.author }}</p>\n        </div>\n\n        <form method="POST">\n            <label for="rating-input">Rating:</label>\n            <select id="rating-input" name="rating">\n                {% for i in range(1,6) %}\n                    <option value="{{ i }}" {% if existing_review and existing_review.rating == i %}selected{% endif %}>{{ i }}</option>\n                {% endfor %}\n            </select>\n\n            <br/>\n            <label for="review-text">Review:</label><br/>\n            <textarea id="review-text" name="review_text" rows="5" cols="40">{% if existing_review %}{{ existing_review.review_text }}{% endif %}</textarea>\n\n            <br/>\n            <button type="submit" id="submit-review-button">Submit Review</button>\n        </form>\n\n        <button id="back-to-book" onclick="window.location.href=\'{{ url_for(\'book_details\', book_id=book.book_id) }}\'">Back to Book</button>\n    </div>\n</body>\n</html>\n\n\n=== design_spec.md ===\n# OnlineLibrary Design Specification\n\n---\n\n## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend Development)\n\n1. **Root Route**\n   - URL Path: `/`\n   - Function Name: `root_redirect`\n   - HTTP Method: GET\n   - Action: Redirects to `/dashboard`\n\n2. **Dashboard Page**\n   - URL Path: `/dashboard`\n   - Function Name: `dashboard`\n   - HTTP Method: GET\n   - Template: `dashboard.html`\n   - Context Variables:\n     - `username` (str) : Current logged-in username\n     - `welcome_message` (str) : Welcome message string\n\n3. **Book Catalog Page**\n   - URL Path: `/catalog`\n   - Function Name: `book_catalog`\n   - HTTP Method: GET\n   - Template: `catalog.html`\n   - Context Variables:\n     - `books` (list of dict) : List of books with keys `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `status`(str)\n     - `search_query` (str) : Current search query (empty string if none)\n\n4. **Book Details Page**\n   - URL Path: `/book/<int:book_id>`\n   - Function Name: `book_details`\n   - HTTP Method: GET\n   - Template: `book_details.html`\n   - Context Variables:\n     - `book` (dict): Book detail with keys `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `status`(str), plus other metadata\n     - `reviews` (list of dict): List of reviews for the book, each with keys `review_id`(int), `username`(str), `rating`(int), `review_text`(str), `review_date`(str)\n     - `username` (str) : Current logged-in user\n\n5. **Borrow Confirmation Page**\n   - URL Path: `/borrow/<int:book_id>`\n   - Function Name: `borrow_confirmation`\n   - HTTP Method: GET, POST\n   - GET Template: `borrow_confirmation.html`\n   - POST: Processes borrow confirmation form submission\n   - Context Variables (GET):\n     - `book` (dict): Book to borrow details\n     - `due_date` (str): Due date string (14 days from borrow date)\n     - `username` (str): Current logged-in user\n\n6. **Borrow Book Action**\n   - URL Path: `/borrow/confirm/<int:book_id>`\n   - Function Name: `confirm_borrow`\n   - HTTP Method: POST\n   - Action: Processes borrow confirmation submission, updates data files\n\n7. **Cancel Borrow Action**\n   - URL Path: `/borrow/cancel/<int:book_id>`\n   - Function Name: `cancel_borrow`\n   - HTTP Method: POST\n   - Action: Redirect back to book details page\n\n8. **My Borrowings Page**\n   - URL Path: `/my-borrows`\n   - Function Name: `my_borrowings`\n   - HTTP Method: GET\n   - Template: `my_borrows.html`\n   - Context Variables:\n     - `borrowings` (list of dict): Borrowed books with keys `borrow_id`(int), `book_title`(str), `borrow_date`(str), `due_date`(str), `status`(str)\n     - `filter_status` (str): Current filter status (All/Active/Returned/Overdue)\n\n9. **Return Book Confirmation Page**\n   - URL Path: `/return/<int:borrow_id>`\n   - Function Name: `return_book_confirmation`\n   - HTTP Method: GET, POST\n   - GET Template: `return_confirmation.html`\n   - POST: Processes book return confirmation\n   - Context Variables (GET):\n     - `borrow` (dict): Borrow record details\n     - `book` (dict): Book details\n     - `username` (str): Current logged-in user\n\n10. **Confirm Return Action**\n    - URL Path: `/return/confirm/<int:borrow_id>`\n    - Function Name: `confirm_return`\n    - HTTP Method: POST\n    - Action: Processes return confirmation, updates data files\n\n11. **Cancel Return Action**\n    - URL Path: `/return/cancel/<int:borrow_id>`\n    - Function Name: `cancel_return`\n    - HTTP Method: POST\n    - Action: Redirect back to My Borrowings page\n\n12. **My Reservations Page**\n    - URL Path: `/my-reservations`\n    - Function Name: `my_reservations`\n    - HTTP Method: GET\n    - Template: `my_reservations.html`\n    - Context Variables:\n      - `reservations` (list of dict): Reservations with keys `reservation_id`(int), `book_title`(str), `reservation_date`(str), `status`(str)\n\n13. **Cancel Reservation Action**\n    - URL Path: `/reservation/cancel/<int:reservation_id>`\n    - Function Name: `cancel_reservation`\n    - HTTP Method: POST\n    - Action: Process cancellation and update data files\n\n14. **My Reviews Page**\n    - URL Path: `/my-reviews`\n    - Function Name: `my_reviews`\n    - HTTP Method: GET\n    - Template: `my_reviews.html`\n    - Context Variables:\n      - `reviews` (list of dict): User reviews with keys `review_id`(int), `book_title`(str), `rating`(int), `review_text`(str)\n\n15. **Write Review Page**\n    - URL Path: `/review/write/<int:book_id>`\n    - Function Name: `write_review`\n    - HTTP Method: GET, POST\n    - GET Template: `write_review.html`\n    - POST: Process review submission\n    - Context Variables (GET):\n      - `book` (dict): Book details\n      - `existing_review` (dict or None): Existing review by user if editing\n\n16. **Edit Review Action**\n    - URL Path: `/review/edit/<int:review_id>`\n    - Function Name: `edit_review`\n    - HTTP Method: GET, POST\n    - GET Template: `write_review.html`\n    - POST: Process editing submission\n    - Context Variables (GET):\n      - `review` (dict): Review details\n      - `book` (dict): Book details\n\n17. **Delete Review Action**\n    - URL Path: `/review/delete/<int:review_id>`\n    - Function Name: `delete_review`\n    - HTTP Method: POST\n    - Action: Process review deletion\n\n18. **User Profile Page**\n    - URL Path: `/profile`\n    - Function Name: `user_profile`\n    - HTTP Method: GET, POST\n    - GET Template: `profile.html`\n    - POST: Process profile update\n    - Context Variables (GET):\n      - `user` (dict): User profile data with keys `username`, `email`, `phone`, `address`\n      - `borrow_history` (list of dict): Past borrowed books with keys `book_title`(str), `borrow_date`(str), `return_date`(str)\n\n19. **Payment Confirmation Page**\n    - URL Path: `/payment/<int:fine_id>`\n    - Function Name: `payment_confirmation`\n    - HTTP Method: GET, POST\n    - GET Template: `payment_confirmation.html`\n    - POST: Process payment confirmation\n    - Context Variables (GET):\n      - `fine` (dict): Fine details with keys `fine_id`(int), `username`(str), `amount`(float), `status`(str)\n\n---\n\n## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (Frontend Development)\n\n### 1. dashboard.html\n- Path: `templates/dashboard.html`\n- Page Title: "Library Dashboard"\n- Elements:\n  - `dashboard-page` (Div)\n  - `welcome-message` (H1) shows welcome message with username\n  - `browse-books-button` (Button) navigates to `book_catalog` route\n  - `my-borrows-button` (Button) navigates to `my_borrowings` route\n- Context Variables:\n  - `username` (str)\n  - `welcome_message` (str)\n- Navigation url_for mappings:\n  - Browse Books Button: `url_for(\'book_catalog\')`\n  - My Borrows Button: `url_for(\'my_borrowings\')`\n\n### 2. catalog.html\n- Path: `templates/catalog.html`\n- Page Title: "Book Catalog"\n- Elements:\n  - `catalog-page` (Div)\n  - `search-input` (Input) for text search\n  - `book-grid` (Div) containing list of books\n  - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (Button) dynamic id per book\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) goes to `dashboard`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `books` (list of dict with keys `book_id`(int), `title`(str), `author`(str), `status`(str))\n  - `search_query` (str)\n- Navigation url_for mappings:\n  - View Book Button: `url_for(\'book_details\', book_id=book.book_id)`\n  - Back to Dashboard: `url_for(\'dashboard\')`\n\n### 3. book_details.html\n- Path: `templates/book_details.html`\n- Page Title: "Book Details"\n- Elements:\n  - `book-details-page` (Div)\n  - `book-title` (H1)\n  - `book-author` (Div)\n  - `book-status` (Div)\n  - `borrow-button` (Button)\n  - `reviews-section` (Div)\n  - `write-review-button` (Button)\n  - `back-to-catalog` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `book` (dict)\n  - `reviews` (list of dict)\n  - `username` (str)\n- Navigation url_for mappings:\n  - Borrow Button: `url_for(\'borrow_confirmation\', book_id=book.book_id)`\n  - Write Review Button: `url_for(\'write_review\', book_id=book.book_id)`\n  - Back to Catalog: `url_for(\'book_catalog\')`\n\n### 4. borrow_confirmation.html\n- Path: `templates/borrow_confirmation.html`\n- Page Title: "Borrow Confirmation"\n- Elements:\n  - `borrow-page` (Div)\n  - `borrow-book-info` (Div)\n  - `due-date-display` (Div)\n  - `confirm-borrow-button` (Button), form method POST, action `/borrow/confirm/<book_id>`\n  - `cancel-borrow-button` (Button), form method POST, action `/borrow/cancel/<book_id>`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `book` (dict)\n  - `due_date` (str)\n  - `username` (str)\n- Navigation url_for mappings:\n  - Cancel Borrow Button: `url_for(\'cancel_borrow\', book_id=book.book_id)`\n\n### 5. my_borrows.html\n- Path: `templates/my_borrows.html`\n- Page Title: "My Borrowings"\n- Elements:\n  - `my-borrows-page` (Div)\n  - `filter-status` (Dropdown) with options All, Active, Returned, Overdue\n  - `borrows-table` (Table)\n  - `return-book-button-{borrow_id}` (Button) dynamic id per active borrow\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `borrowings` (list of dict)\n  - `filter_status` (str)\n- Navigation url_for mappings:\n  - Return Book Button: `url_for(\'return_book_confirmation\', borrow_id=borrow.borrow_id)`\n  - Back to Dashboard: `url_for(\'dashboard\')`\n\n### 6. return_confirmation.html\n- Path: `templates/return_confirmation.html`\n- Page Title: "Return Confirmation"\n- Elements:\n  - `return-confirmation-page` (Div) (container assumed)\n  - `borrow-info` (Div) (shows borrow details)\n  - `confirm-return-button` (Button), form method POST, action `/return/confirm/<borrow_id>`\n  - `cancel-return-button` (Button), form method POST, action `/return/cancel/<borrow_id>`\n- Context Variables:\n  - `borrow` (dict)\n  - `book` (dict)\n  - `username` (str)\n- Navigation url_for mappings:\n  - Cancel Return Button: `url_for(\'cancel_return\', borrow_id=borrow.borrow_id)`\n\n### 7. my_reservations.html\n- Path: `templates/my_reservations.html`\n- Page Title: "My Reservations"\n- Elements:\n  - `reservations-page` (Div)\n  - `reservations-table` (Table)\n  - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` (Button) dynamic id per reservation\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `reservations` (list of dict)\n- Navigation url_for mappings:\n  - Cancel Reservation Button: `url_for(\'cancel_reservation\', reservation_id=reservation.reservation_id)`\n  - Back to Dashboard: `url_for(\'dashboard\')`\n\n### 8. my_reviews.html\n- Path: `templates/my_reviews.html`\n- Page Title: "My Reviews"\n- Elements:\n  - `reviews-page` (Div)\n  - `reviews-list` (Div)\n  - `edit-review-button-{review_id}` (Button), dynamic id per review\n  - `delete-review-button-{review_id}` (Button), dynamic id per review\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `reviews` (list of dict)\n- Navigation url_for mappings:\n  - Edit Review Button: `url_for(\'edit_review\', review_id=review.review_id)`\n  - Delete Review Button: `url_for(\'delete_review\', review_id=review.review_id)`\n  - Back to Dashboard: `url_for(\'dashboard\')`\n\n### 9. write_review.html\n- Path: `templates/write_review.html`\n- Page Title: "Write Review"\n- Elements:\n  - `write-review-page` (Div)\n  - `book-info-display` (Div)\n  - `rating-input` (Dropdown), options 1 to 5\n  - `review-text` (Textarea)\n  - `submit-review-button` (Button), form method POST\n  - `back-to-book` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `book` (dict)\n  - `existing_review` (dict or None)\n- Navigation url_for mappings:\n  - Back to Book: `url_for(\'book_details\', book_id=book.book_id)`\n\n### 10. profile.html\n- Path: `templates/profile.html`\n- Page Title: "My Profile"\n- Elements:\n  - `profile-page` (Div)\n  - `profile-username` (Div)\n  - `profile-email` (Input)\n  - `update-profile-button` (Button), form method POST\n  - `borrow-history` (Div)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `user` (dict) with keys: `username`(str), `email`(str), `phone`(str), `address`(str)\n  - `borrow_history` (list of dict) with keys: `book_title`(str), `borrow_date`(str), `return_date`(str or empty)\n- Navigation url_for mappings:\n  - Back to Dashboard: `url_for(\'dashboard\')`\n\n### 11. payment_confirmation.html\n- Path: `templates/payment_confirmation.html`\n- Page Title: "Payment Confirmation"\n- Elements:\n  - `payment-page` (Div)\n  - `fine-amount-display` (Div)\n  - `confirm-payment-button` (Button), form method POST\n  - `back-to-profile` (Button)\n- Context Variables:\n  - `fine` (dict) with keys: `fine_id`(int), `username`(str), `amount`(float), `status`(str)\n- Navigation url_for mappings:\n  - Back to Profile: `url_for(\'user_profile\')`\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas (Backend Development)\n\n### 1. users.txt\n- Path: `data/users.txt`\n- Fields (pipe-delimited):\n  - `username` (str)\n  - `email` (str)\n  - `phone` (str)\n  - `address` (str)\n- Data Description: User profile information including contact details.\n- Example Rows:\n  - `john_reader|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St`\n  - `jane_doe|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak St`\n- Parsing Notes: Fields are strings; no headers included.\n\n### 2. books.txt\n- Path: `data/books.txt`\n- Fields (pipe-delimited):\n  - `book_id` (int)\n  - `title` (str)\n  - `author` (str)\n  - `isbn` (str)\n  - `genre` (str)\n  - `publisher` (str)\n  - `year` (int)\n  - `description` (str)\n  - `status` (str) - One of: Available, Borrowed, Reserved\n  - `avg_rating` (float)\n- Data Description: Information about books including status and average rating.\n- Example Rows:\n  - `1|To Kill a Mockingbird|Harper Lee|978-0-06-112008-4|Fiction|HarperCollins|1960|A gripping tale of racial injustice and childhood innocence.|Available|4.8`\n  - `2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|978-0-06-231609-7|Non-Fiction|Harper|2011|A brief history of humankind.|Borrowed|4.6`\n  - `3|1984|George Orwell|978-0-452-28423-4|Fiction|Signet Classic|1949|A dystopian social science fiction novel.|Available|4.7`\n  - `4|The Selfish Gene|Richard Dawkins|978-0-19-286092-7|Science|Oxford University Press|1976|Gene-centered view of evolution.|Reserved|4.5`\n  - `5|Steve Jobs|Walter Isaacson|978-1-4516-4853-9|Biography|Simon & Schuster|2011|Biography of Apple co-founder.|Available|4.3`\n- Parsing Notes: `book_id` and `year` are integers, `avg_rating` is float.\n\n### 3. borrowings.txt\n- Path: `data/borrowings.txt`\n- Fields (pipe-delimited):\n  - `borrow_id` (int)\n  - `username` (str)\n  - `book_id` (int)\n  - `borrow_date` (str, format YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - `due_date` (str, format YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - `return_date` (str or empty)\n  - `status` (str) - One of: Active, Returned, Overdue\n  - `fine_amount` (float)\n- Data Description: Records of borrowed books including dates, status, and fines.\n- Example Rows:\n  - `1|john_reader|2|2024-11-01|2024-11-15||Active|0`\n  - `2|jane_doe|1|2024-10-20|2024-11-03|2024-11-02|Returned|0`\n  - `3|john_reader|3|2024-10-15|2024-10-29||Overdue|5.00`\n- Parsing Notes: `borrow_id`, `book_id` integers; `fine_amount` float; dates as string.\n\n### 4. reservations.txt\n- Path: `data/reservations.txt`\n- Fields (pipe-delimited):\n  - `reservation_id` (int)\n  - `username` (str)\n  - `book_id` (int)\n  - `reservation_date` (str, format YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - `status` (str) - One of: Active, Cancelled\n- Data Description: Book reservation records with status tracking.\n- Example Rows:\n  - `1|jane_doe|4|2024-11-10|Active`\n  - `2|john_reader|2|2024-10-25|Cancelled`\n- Parsing Notes: `reservation_id`, `book_id` integers; date as string.\n\n### 5. reviews.txt\n- Path: `data/reviews.txt`\n- Fields (pipe-delimited):\n  - `review_id` (int)\n  - `username` (str)\n  - `book_id` (int)\n  - `rating` (int) (1 to 5)\n  - `review_text` (str)\n  - `review_date` (str, format YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Data Description: User submitted book reviews.\n- Example Rows:\n  - `1|jane_doe|1|5|An absolute masterpiece! Borrow Confirmation page (GET for form display, POST to process borrow) @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def borrow_confirmation(book_id):     books = load_books()     book = books.get(book_id)     if not book:         flash('Book not found', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))      username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      if request.method == 'GET':         # Show confirmation page         borrow_date_obj = datetime.today()         due_date_obj = borrow_date_obj + timedelta(days=14)         due_date = due_date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')         return render_template('borrow_confirmation.html', book=book, due_date=due_date, username=username)      elif request.method == 'POST':         # Not allowed here; borrow confirm is in different route         return redirect(url_for('confirm_borrow', book_id=book_id))  # 6. Borrow Book Action (POST) @app.route('/borrow/confirm/<int:book_id>', methods=['POST']) def confirm_borrow(book_id):     books = load_books()     borrowings = load_borrowings()      book = books.get(book_id)     if not book:         flash('Book not found', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))      username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      # Check if book is available     if book['status'] != 'Available':         flash('Book is not available for borrowing.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))      # Check if user already has borrowed this book and not returned     user_active_borrows = [b for b in borrowings.values() if b['username'] == username and b['book_id'] == book_id and b['status'] == 'Active']     if user_active_borrows:         flash('You already have this book borrowed.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))      # Generate new borrow_id     new_borrow_id = max(borrowings.keys(), default=0) + 1      borrow_date = datetime.today()     due_date = borrow_date + timedelta(days=14)      # New borrow record     borrow_record = {         'borrow_id': new_borrow_id,         'username': username,         'book_id': book_id,         'borrow_date': borrow_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d'),         'due_date': due_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d'),         'return_date': '',         'status': 'Active',         'fine_amount': 0.0     }      borrowings[new_borrow_id] = borrow_record      # Mark book as Borrowed     book['status'] = 'Borrowed'      # Save updates     save_borrowings(borrowings)     save_books(books)      flash('Borrow confirmed successfully.', 'success')     return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))  # 7. My Borrowings page @app.route('/my-borrows') def my_borrowings():     borrowings = load_borrowings()     books = load_books()     username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      filter_status = request.args.get('filter', 'All')      user_borrows = [b for b in borrowings.values() if b['username'] == username]      # Update borrowing statuses for overdue     today = datetime.today().date()     changed = False     for b in user_borrows:         if b['status'] == 'Active':             due_date_obj = datetime.strptime(b['due_date'], '%Y-%m-%d').date()             if due_date_obj < today:                 b['status'] = 'Overdue'                 # Add fine if not already added                 if b['fine_amount'] == 0:                     b['fine_amount'] = 5.0  # Flat fine amount                     changed = True     if changed:         # Save borrowings updates         save_borrowings(borrowings)      if filter_status != 'All':         user_borrows = [b for b in user_borrows if b['status'] == filter_status]      borrows_display = []     for b in user_borrows:         borrows_display.append({             'borrow_id': b['borrow_id'],             'book_title': books[b['book_id']]['title'] if b['book_id'] in books else 'Unknown',             'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],             'due_date': b['due_date'],             'status': b['status']         })      return render_template('my_borrows.html', borrowings=borrows_display, filter_status=filter_status)  # 9. Return Book Confirmation page @app.route('/return/<int:borrow_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def return_book_confirmation(borrow_id):     borrowings = load_borrowings()     books = load_books()     borrow = borrowings.get(borrow_id)     if not borrow:         flash('Borrow record not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))      book = books.get(borrow['book_id'], None)     if book is None:         flash('Book record not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))      username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      if request.method == 'GET':         return render_template('return_confirmation.html', borrow=borrow, book=book, username=username)      if request.method == 'POST':         return redirect(url_for('confirm_return', borrow_id=borrow_id))  # 10. Confirm Return Action @app.route('/return/confirm/<int:borrow_id>', methods=['POST']) def confirm_return(borrow_id):     borrowings = load_borrowings()     books = load_books()     fines = load_fines()      borrow = borrowings.get(borrow_id)     if not borrow:         flash('Borrow record not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))      book = books.get(borrow['book_id'])     if not book:         flash('Book record not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))      username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      # Only Active or Overdue can be returned     if borrow['status'] not in ['Active', 'Overdue']:         flash('This borrow record cannot be returned.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))      return_date = datetime.today()     borrow['return_date'] = return_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')     borrow['status'] = 'Returned'      # Update book status     book['status'] = 'Available'      # If borrow was overdue and fine_amount > 0 create fine record if not exist     if borrow['status'] == 'Returned' and borrow['fine_amount'] > 0:         # Check if fine already exists         existing_fine = None         for fine in fines.values():             if fine['borrow_id'] == borrow_id:                 existing_fine = fine                 break         if not existing_fine:             new_fine_id = max(fines.keys(), default=0) + 1             fine_record = {                 'fine_id': new_fine_id,                 'username': username,                 'borrow_id': borrow_id,                 'amount': borrow['fine_amount'],                 'status': 'Unpaid',                 'date_issued': return_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')             }             fines[new_fine_id] = fine_record             save_fines(fines)      save_borrowings(borrowings)     save_books(books)      flash('Book returned successfully.', 'success')     return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))  # 11. My Reservations Page @app.route('/my-reservations') def my_reservations():     reservations = load_reservations()     books = load_books()     username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      user_reservations = [r for r in reservations.values() if r['username'] == username and r['status'] == 'Active']      res_display = []     for r in user_reservations:         res_display.append({             'reservation_id': r['reservation_id'],             'book_title': books[r['book_id']]['title'] if r['book_id'] in books else 'Unknown',             'reservation_date': r['reservation_date'],             'status': r['status']         })      return render_template('my_reservations.html', reservations=res_display)  # 13. Cancel Reservation Action @app.route('/reservation/cancel/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['POST']) def cancel_reservation(reservation_id):     reservations = load_reservations()     reservation = reservations.get(reservation_id)     if not reservation:         flash('Reservation not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_reservations'))      if reservation['status'] != 'Active':         flash('Reservation is not active.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_reservations'))      reservation['status'] = 'Cancelled'     save_reservations(reservations)      flash('Reservation cancelled successfully.', 'success')     return redirect(url_for('my_reservations'))  # 14. My Reviews page @app.route('/my-reviews') def my_reviews():     reviews = load_reviews()     books = load_books()     username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      user_reviews = [r for r in reviews.values() if r['username'] == username]      reviews_display = []     for r in user_reviews:         reviews_display.append({             'review_id': r['review_id'],             'book_title': books[r['book_id']]['title'] if r['book_id'] in books else 'Unknown',             'rating': r['rating'],             'review_text': r['review_text']         })      return render_template('my_reviews.html', reviews=reviews_display)  # 15. Write Review page (GET and POST) @app.route('/review/write/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def write_review(book_id):     books = load_books()     book = books.get(book_id)     if not book:         flash('Book not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))      reviews = load_reviews()     username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      # Check for existing review by user for this book     existing_review = None     for review in reviews.values():         if review['username'] == username and review['book_id'] == book_id:             existing_review = review             break      if request.method == 'GET':         return render_template('write_review.html', book=book, existing_review=existing_review)      if request.method == 'POST':         rating = int(request.form.get('rating', '0'))         review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()         if rating < 1 or rating > 5:             flash('Rating must be between 1 and 5.', 'error')             return redirect(url_for('write_review', book_id=book_id))         if not review_text:             flash('Review text cannot be empty.', 'error')             return redirect(url_for('write_review', book_id=book_id))          review_date = datetime.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')          if existing_review:             # Update existing review             existing_review['rating'] = rating             existing_review['review_text'] = review_text             existing_review['review_date'] = review_date         else:             # Add new review             new_review_id = max(reviews.keys(), default=0) + 1             new_review = {                 'review_id': new_review_id,                 'username': username,                 'book_id': book_id,                 'rating': rating,                 'review_text': review_text,                 'review_date': review_date             }             reviews[new_review_id] = new_review          # Save reviews         save_reviews(reviews)          # Update avg_rating in book         book_reviews = [r for r in reviews.values() if r['book_id'] == book_id]         if book_reviews:             avg_rating = sum(r['rating'] for r in book_reviews) / len(book_reviews)             book['avg_rating'] = round(avg_rating, 1)         else:             book['avg_rating'] = 0.0         save_books(books)          flash('Review submitted successfully.', 'success')         return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))  # 16. Edit Review Action (GET and POST) @app.route('/review/edit/<int:review_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def edit_review(review_id):     reviews = load_reviews()     review = reviews.get(review_id)     if not review:         flash('Review not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))      books = load_books()     book = books.get(review['book_id'])     if not book:         flash('Book for review not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))      username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME     if review['username'] != username:         flash('You can only edit your own reviews.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))      if request.method == 'GET':         return render_template('write_review.html', review=review, book=book)      if request.method == 'POST':         rating = int(request.form.get('rating', '0'))         review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()          if rating < 1 or rating > 5:             flash('Rating must be between 1 and 5.', 'error')             return redirect(url_for('edit_review', review_id=review_id))         if not review_text:             flash('Review text cannot be empty.', 'error')             return redirect(url_for('edit_review', review_id=review_id))          review['rating'] = rating         review['review_text'] = review_text         review['review_date'] = datetime.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')          save_reviews(reviews)          # Update avg_rating in book         book_reviews = [r for r in reviews.values() if r['book_id'] == book['book_id']]         if book_reviews:             avg_rating = sum(r['rating'] for r in book_reviews) / len(book_reviews)             book['avg_rating'] = round(avg_rating, 1)         else:             book['avg_rating'] = 0.0         save_books(books)          flash('Review edited successfully.', 'success')         return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))  # 17. Delete Review Action (POST) @app.route('/review/delete/<int:review_id>', methods=['POST']) def delete_review(review_id):     reviews = load_reviews()     review = reviews.get(review_id)     if not review:         flash('Review not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))      username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME     if review['username'] != username:         flash('You can only delete your own reviews.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))      book_id = review['book_id']     del reviews[review_id]     save_reviews(reviews)      # Update avg_rating in book     books = load_books()     book = books.get(book_id)     if book:         book_reviews = [r for r in reviews.values() if r['book_id'] == book_id]         if book_reviews:             avg_rating = sum(r['rating'] for r in book_reviews) / len(book_reviews)             book['avg_rating'] = round(avg_rating, 1)         else:             book['avg_rating'] = 0.0         save_books(books)      flash('Review deleted successfully.', 'success')     return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))  # 18. User Profile Page (GET and POST) @app.route('/profile', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def user_profile():     users = load_users()     username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      if username not in users:         flash('User profile not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))      user = users[username]     borrowings = load_borrowings()     books = load_books()      if request.method == 'GET':         # Prepare borrow history         borrow_history = []         for b in borrowings.values():             if b['username'] == username:                 book_title = books[b['book_id']]['title'] if b['book_id'] in books else 'Unknown'                 borrow_history.append({                     'book_title': book_title,                     'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],                     'return_date': b['return_date'] if b['return_date'] else ''                 })         return render_template('profile.html', user=user, borrow_history=borrow_history)      if request.method == 'POST':         # Process profile update         email = request.form.get('email', '').strip()         phone = request.form.get('phone', '').strip()         address = request.form.get('address', '').strip()          if not email or not phone or not address:             flash('All fields are required.', 'error')             return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))          user['email'] = email         user['phone'] = phone         user['address'] = address          users[username] = user         save_users(users)          flash('Profile updated successfully.', 'success')         return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))  # 19. Payment Confirmation page (GET and POST) @app.route('/payment/<int:fine_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def payment_confirmation(fine_id):     fines = load_fines()     fine = fines.get(fine_id)     if not fine:         flash('Fine record not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))      username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      if fine['username'] != username:         flash('You can only pay your own fines.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))      if request.method == 'GET':         return render_template('payment_confirmation.html', fine=fine)      if request.method == 'POST':         # Process payment         if fine['status'] == 'Paid':             flash('Fine is already paid.', 'info')             return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))          fine['status'] = 'Paid'         fines[fine_id] = fine         save_fines(fines)          flash('Payment processed successfully.', 'success')         return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))   if __name__ == '__main__':     app.run(debug=True)

print(f\"Error saving reviews: {e}\")\n\n\ndef load_fines():\n    fines = {}\n    try:\n        with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'fines.txt'), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            for line in Book Catalog page\n@app.route('/catalog')\ndef book_catalog():\n    books = load_books()\n    search_query = request.args.get('q', '').strip()\n    book_list = list(books.values())\n    if search_query:\n        sq = search_query.lower()\n        book_list = [b for b in book_list if sq in b['title'].lower() or sq in b['author'].lower()]\n    return render_template('catalog.html', books=book_list, search_query=search_query)\n\n# 4. Borrow Confirmation page (GET for form display, POST to process borrow)\n@app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef borrow_confirmation(book_id):\n    books = load_books()\n    book = books.get(book_id)\n    if not book:\n        flash('Book not found', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))\n\n    username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME\n\n    if request.method == 'GET':\n        # Show confirmation page\n        borrow_date_obj = datetime.today()\n        due_date_obj = borrow_date_obj + timedelta(days=14)\n        due_date = due_date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n        return render_template('borrow_confirmation.html', book=book, due_date=due_date, username=username)\n\n    elif request.method == 'POST':\n        # Not allowed here; borrow confirm is in different route\n        return redirect(url_for('confirm_borrow', book_id=book_id))\n\n# 6. Borrow Book Action (POST)\n@app.route('/borrow/confirm/<int:book_id>', methods=['POST'])\ndef confirm_borrow(book_id):\n    books = load_books()\n    borrowings = load_borrowings()\n\n    book = books.get(book_id)\n    if not book:\n        flash('Book not found', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))\n\n    username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME\n\n    # Check if book is available\n    if book['status'] != 'Available':\n        flash('Book is not available for borrowing.', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))\n\n    # Check if user already has borrowed this book and not returned\n    user_active_borrows = [b for b in borrowings.values() if b['username'] == username and b['book_id'] == book_id and b['status'] == 'Active']\n    if user_active_borrows:\n        flash('You already have this book borrowed.', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))\n\n    # Generate new borrow_id\n    new_borrow_id = max(borrowings.keys(), default=0) + 1\n\n    borrow_date = datetime.today()\n    due_date = borrow_date + timedelta(days=14)\n\n    # New borrow record\n    borrow_record = {\n        'borrow_id': new_borrow_id,\n        'username': username,\n        'book_id': book_id,\n        'borrow_date': borrow_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d'),\n        'due_date': due_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d'),\n        'return_date': '',\n        'status': 'Active',\n        'fine_amount': 0.0\n    }\n\n    borrowings[new_borrow_id] = borrow_record\n\n    # Mark book as Borrowed\n    book['status'] = 'Borrowed'\n\n    # Save updates\n    save_borrowings(borrowings)\n    save_books(books)\n\n    flash('Borrow confirmed successfully.', 'success')\n    return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))\n\n# 7. Cancel Borrow Action (POST)\n@app.route('/borrow/cancel/<int:book_id>', methods=['POST'])\ndef cancel_borrow(book_id):\n    return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))\n\n# 8. My Borrowings page\n@app.route('/my-borrows')\ndef my_borrowings():\n    borrowings = load_borrowings()\n    books = load_books()\n    username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME\n\n    filter_status = request.args.get('filter', 'All')\n\n    user_borrows = [b for b in borrowings.values() if b['username'] == username]\n\n    # Update borrowing statuses for overdue\n    today = datetime.today().date()\n    changed = False\n    for b in user_borrows:\n        if b['status'] == 'Active':\n            due_date_obj = datetime.strptime(b['due_date'], '%Y-%m-%d').date()\n            if due_date_obj < today:\n                b['status'] = 'Overdue'\n                # Add fine if not already added\n                if b['fine_amount'] == 0:\n                    b['fine_amount'] = 5.0  # Flat fine amount\n                    changed = True\n    if changed:\n        # Save borrowings updates\n        save_borrowings(borrowings)\n\n    if filter_status != 'All':\n        user_borrows = [b for b in user_borrows if b['status'] == filter_status]\n\n    borrows_display = []\n    for b in user_borrows:\n        borrows_display.append({\n            'borrow_id': b['borrow_id'],\n            'book_title': books[b['book_id']]['title'] if b['book_id'] in books else 'Unknown',\n            'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],\n            'due_date': b['due_date'],\n            'status': b['status']\n        })\n\n    return render_template('my_borrows.html', borrowings=borrows_display, filter_status=filter_status)\n\n# 9. Return Book Confirmation page\n@app.route('/return/<int:borrow_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef return_book_confirmation(borrow_id):\n    borrowings = load_borrowings()\n    books = load_books()\n    borrow = borrowings.get(borrow_id)\n    if not borrow:\n        flash('Borrow record not found.', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))\n\n    book = books.get(borrow['book_id'], None)\n    if book is None:\n        flash('Book record not found.', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('my_borrows'))\n\n    username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME\n\n    if request.method == 'GET':\n        return render_template('return_confirmation.html', borrow=borrow, book=book, username=username)\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        return redirect(url_for('confirm_return', borrow_id=borrow_id))\n\n# 10. Confirm Return Action\n@app.route('/return/confirm/<int:borrow_id>', methods=['POST'])\ndef confirm_return(borrow_id):\n    borrowings = load_borrowings()\n    books = load_books()\n    fines = load_fines()\n\n    borrow = borrowings.get(borrow_id)\n    if not borrow:\n        flash('Borrow record not found.', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))\n\n    book = books.get(borrow['book_id'])\n    if not book:\n        flash('Book record not found.', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))\n\n    username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME\n\n    # Only Active or Overdue can be returned\n    if borrow['status'] not in ['Active', 'Overdue']:\n        flash('This borrow record cannot be returned.', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))\n\n    return_date = datetime.today()\n    is_overdue = (borrow['status'] == 'Overdue')\n\n    borrow['return_date'] = return_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n    borrow['status'] = 'Returned'\n\n    # Update book status\n    book['status'] = 'Available'\n\n    # If borrow was overdue and fine_amount > 0 create fine record if not exist\n    if is_overdue and borrow['fine_amount'] > 0:\n        # Check if fine already exists\n        existing_fine = None\n        for fine in fines.values():\n            if fine['borrow_id'] == borrow_id:\n                existing_fine = fine\n                break\n        if not existing_fine:\n            new_fine_id = max(fines.keys(), default=0) + 1\n            fine_record = {\n                'fine_id': new_fine_id,\n                'username': username,\n                'borrow_id': borrow_id,\n                'amount': borrow['fine_amount'],\n                'status': 'Unpaid',\n                'date_issued': return_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n            }\n            fines[new_fine_id] = fine_record\n            save_fines(fines)\n\n    save_borrowings(borrowings)\n    save_books(books)\n\n    flash('Book returned successfully.', 'success')\n    return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))\n\n# 11. My Reviews page\n@app.route('/my-reviews')\ndef my_reviews():\n    reviews = load_reviews()\n    books = load_books()\n    username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME\n\n    user_reviews = [r for r in reviews.values() if r['username'] == username]\n\n    reviews_display = []\n    for r in user_reviews:\n        reviews_display.append({\n            'review_id': r['review_id'],\n            'book_title': books[r['book_id']]['title'] if r['book_id'] in books else 'Unknown',\n            'rating': r['rating'],\n            'review_text': r['review_text']\n        })\n\n    return render_template('my_reviews.html', reviews=reviews_display)\n\n# 15. Write Review page (GET and POST)\n@app.route('/review/write/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef write_review(book_id):\n    books = load_books()\n    book = books.get(book_id)\n    if not book:\n        flash('Book not found.', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))\n\n    reviews = load_reviews()\n    username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME\n\n    # Check for existing review by user for this book\n    existing_review = None\n    for review in reviews.values():\n        if review['username'] == username and review['book_id'] == book_id:\n            existing_review = review\n            break\n\n    if request.method == 'GET':\n        return render_template('write_review.html', book=book, existing_review=existing_review)\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        rating = int(request.form.get('rating', '0'))\n        review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()\n        if rating < 1 or rating > 5:\n            flash('Rating must be between 1 and 5.', 'error')\n            return redirect(url_for('write_review', book_id=book_id))\n        if not review_text:\n            flash('Review text cannot be empty.', 'error')\n            return redirect(url_for('write_review', book_id=book_id))\n\n        review_date = datetime.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n\n        if existing_review:\n            # Update existing review\n            existing_review['rating'] = rating\n            existing_review['review_text'] = review_text\n            existing_review['review_date'] = review_date\n        else:\n            # Add new review\n            new_review_id = max(reviews.keys(), default=0) + 1\n            new_review = {\n                'review_id': new_review_id,\n                'username': username,\n                'book_id': book_id,\n                'rating': rating,\n                'review_text': review_text,\n                'review_date': review_date\n            }\n            reviews[new_review_id] = new_review\n\n        # Save reviews\n        save_reviews(reviews)\n\n        # Update avg_rating in book\n        book_reviews = [r for r in reviews.values() if r['book_id'] == book_id]\n        if book_reviews:\n            avg_rating = sum(r['rating'] for r in book_reviews) / len(book_reviews)\n            book['avg_rating'] = round(avg_rating, 1)\n        else:\n            book['avg_rating'] = 0.0\n        save_books(books)\n\n        flash('Review submitted successfully.', 'success')\n        return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))\n\n# 16. Edit Review Action (GET and POST)\n@app.route('/review/edit/<int:review_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef edit_review(review_id):\n    reviews = load_reviews()\n    review = reviews.get(review_id)\n    if not review:\n        flash('Review not found.', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))\n\n    books = load_books()\n    book = books.get(review['book_id'])\n    if not book:\n        flash('Book for review not found.', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))\n\n    username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME\n    if review['username'] != username:\n        flash('You can only edit your own reviews.', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))\n\n    if request.method == 'GET':\n        return render_template('write_review.html', existing_review=review, book=book)\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        rating = int(request.form.get('rating', '0'))\n        review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()\n\n        if rating < 1 or rating > 5:\n            flash('Rating must be between 1 and 5.', 'error')\n            return redirect(url_for('edit_review', review_id=review_id))\n        if not review_text:\n            flash('Review text cannot be empty.', 'error')\n            return redirect(url_for('edit_review', review_id=review_id))\n\n        review['rating'] = rating\n        review['review_text'] = review_text\n        review['review_date'] = datetime.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n\n        save_reviews(reviews)\n\n        # Update avg_rating in book\n        book_reviews = [r for r in reviews.values() if r['book_id'] == book['book_id']]\n        if book_reviews:\n            avg_rating = sum(r['rating'] for r in book_reviews) / len(book_reviews)\n            book['avg_rating'] = round(avg_rating, 1)\n        else:\n            book['avg_rating'] = 0.0\n        save_books(books)\n\n        flash('Review edited successfully.', 'success')\n        return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))\n\n# 17. Delete Review Action (POST)\n@app.route('/review/delete/<int:review_id>', methods=['POST'])\ndef delete_review(review_id):\n    reviews = load_reviews()\n    review = reviews.get(review_id)\n    if not review:\n        flash('Review not found.', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))\n\n    username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME\n    if review['username'] != username:\n        flash('You can only delete your own reviews.', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))\n\n    book_id = review['book_id']\n    del reviews[review_id]\n    save_reviews(reviews)\n\n    # Update avg_rating in book\n    books = load_books()\n    book = books.get(book_id)\n    if book:\n        book_reviews = [r for r in reviews.values() if r['book_id'] == book_id]\n        if book_reviews:\n            avg_rating = sum(r['rating'] for r in book_reviews) / len(book_reviews)\n            book['avg_rating'] = round(avg_rating, 1)\n        else:\n            book['avg_rating'] = 0.0\n        save_books(books)\n\n    flash('Review deleted successfully.', 'success')\n    return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))\n\n# 18. User Profile Page (GET and POST)\n@app.route('/profile', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef user_profile():\n    users = load_users()\n    username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME\n\n    if username not in users:\n        flash('User profile not found.', 'error')\n        return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))\n\n    user = users[username]\n    borrowings = load_borrowings()\n    books = load_books()\n\n    if request.method == 'GET':\n        # Prepare borrow history\n        borrow_history = []\n        for b in borrowings.values():\n            if b['username'] == username:\n                book_title = books[b['book_id']]['title'] if b['book_id'] in books else 'Unknown'\n                borrow_history.append({\n                    'book_title': book_title,\n                    'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],\n                    'return_date': b['return_date'] if b['return_date'] else ''\n                })\n        return render_template('profile.html', user=user, borrow_history=borrow_history)\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        # Process profile update\n        email = request.form.get('email', '').strip()\n        phone = request.form.get('phone', '').strip()\n        address = request.form.get('address', '').strip()\n\n        if not email or not phone or not address:\n            flash('All fields are required.', 'error')\n            return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))\n\n        user['email'] = email\n        user['phone'] = phone\n        user['address'] = address\n\n        users[username] = user\n        save_users(users)\n\n        flash('Profile updated successfully.', 'success')\n        return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))\n\n# 19. Root route: redirects to /dashboard @app.route('/') def root_redirect():     return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))  # 2. Dashboard page @app.route('/dashboard') def dashboard():     username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME     welcome_message = f"Welcome back, {username}!"     return render_template('dashboard.html', username=username, welcome_message=welcome_message)  # 3. Book Catalog page @app.route('/catalog') def book_catalog():     books = load_books()     search_query = request.args.get('q', '').strip()     book_list = list(books.values())     if search_query:         sq = search_query.lower()         book_list = [b for b in book_list if sq in b['title'].lower() or sq in b['author'].lower()]     return render_template('catalog.html', books=book_list, search_query=search_query)  # 4. Book Details page @app.route('/book/<int:book_id>') def book_details(book_id):     books = load_books()     book = books.get(book_id)     if not book:         flash('Book not found', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))     reviews_all = load_reviews()     reviews = [r for r in reviews_all.values() if r['book_id'] == book_id]     username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME     return render_template('book_details.html', book=book, reviews=reviews, username=username)  # 5. Borrow Confirmation page (GET for form display, POST to process borrow) @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def borrow_confirmation(book_id):     books = load_books()     book = books.get(book_id)     if not book:         flash('Book not found', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))      username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      if request.method == 'GET':         # Show confirmation page         borrow_date_obj = datetime.today()         due_date_obj = borrow_date_obj + timedelta(days=14)         due_date = due_date_obj.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')         return render_template('borrow_confirmation.html', book=book, due_date=due_date, username=username)      elif request.method == 'POST':         # Not allowed here; borrow confirm is in different route         return redirect(url_for('confirm_borrow', book_id=book_id))  # 6. Borrow Book Action (POST) @app.route('/borrow/confirm/<int:book_id>', methods=['POST']) def confirm_borrow(book_id):     books = load_books()     borrowings = load_borrowings()      book = books.get(book_id)     if not book:         flash('Book not found', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))      username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      # Check if book is available     if book['status'] != 'Available':         flash('Book is not available for borrowing.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))      # Check if user already has borrowed this book and not returned     user_active_borrows = [b for b in borrowings.values() if b['username'] == username and b['book_id'] == book_id and b['status'] == 'Active']     if user_active_borrows:         flash('You already have this book borrowed.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))      # Generate new borrow_id     new_borrow_id = max(borrowings.keys(), default=0) + 1      borrow_date = datetime.today()     due_date = borrow_date + timedelta(days=14)      # New borrow record     borrow_record = {         'borrow_id': new_borrow_id,         'username': username,         'book_id': book_id,         'borrow_date': borrow_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d'),         'due_date': due_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d'),         'return_date': '',         'status': 'Active',         'fine_amount': 0.0     }      borrowings[new_borrow_id] = borrow_record      # Mark book as Borrowed     book['status'] = 'Borrowed'      # Save updates     save_borrowings(borrowings)     save_books(books)      flash('Borrow confirmed successfully.', 'success')     return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))  # 7. Cancel Borrow Action (POST) @app.route('/borrow/cancel/<int:book_id>', methods=['POST']) def cancel_borrow(book_id):     return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))  # 8. My Borrowings page @app.route('/my-borrows') def my_borrowings():     borrowings = load_borrowings()     books = load_books()     username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      filter_status = request.args.get('filter', 'All')      user_borrows = [b for b in borrowings.values() if b['username'] == username]      # Update borrowing statuses for overdue     today = datetime.today().date()     changed = False     for b in user_borrows:         if b['status'] == 'Active':             due_date_obj = datetime.strptime(b['due_date'], '%Y-%m-%d').date()             if due_date_obj < today:                 b['status'] = 'Overdue'                 # Add fine if not already added                 if b['fine_amount'] == 0:                     b['fine_amount'] = 5.0  # Flat fine amount                     changed = True     if changed:         # Save borrowings updates         save_borrowings(borrowings)      if filter_status != 'All':         user_borrows = [b for b in user_borrows if b['status'] == filter_status]      borrows_display = []     for b in user_borrows:         borrows_display.append({             'borrow_id': b['borrow_id'],             'book_title': books[b['book_id']]['title'] if b['book_id'] in books else 'Unknown',             'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],             'due_date': b['due_date'],             'status': b['status']         })      return render_template('my_borrows.html', borrowings=borrows_display, filter_status=filter_status)  # 9. Return Book Confirmation page @app.route('/return/<int:borrow_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def return_book_confirmation(borrow_id):     borrowings = load_borrowings()     books = load_books()     borrow = borrowings.get(borrow_id)     if not borrow:         flash('Borrow record not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))      book = books.get(borrow['book_id'], None)     if book is None:         flash('Book record not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_borrows'))      username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      if request.method == 'GET':         return render_template('return_confirmation.html', borrow=borrow, book=book, username=username)      if request.method == 'POST':         return redirect(url_for('confirm_return', borrow_id=borrow_id))  # 10. Confirm Return Action @app.route('/return/confirm/<int:borrow_id>', methods=['POST']) def confirm_return(borrow_id):     borrowings = load_borrowings()     books = load_books()     fines = load_fines()      borrow = borrowings.get(borrow_id)     if not borrow:         flash('Borrow record not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))      book = books.get(borrow['book_id'])     if not book:         flash('Book record not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))      username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      # Only Active or Overdue can be returned     if borrow['status'] not in ['Active', 'Overdue']:         flash('This borrow record cannot be returned.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))      return_date = datetime.today()     is_overdue = (borrow['status'] == 'Overdue')      borrow['return_date'] = return_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')     borrow['status'] = 'Returned'      # Update book status     book['status'] = 'Available'      # If borrow was overdue and fine_amount > 0 create fine record if not exist     if is_overdue and borrow['fine_amount'] > 0:         # Check if fine already exists         existing_fine = None         for fine in fines.values():             if fine['borrow_id'] == borrow_id:                 existing_fine = fine                 break         if not existing_fine:             new_fine_id = max(fines.keys(), default=0) + 1             fine_record = {                 'fine_id': new_fine_id,                 'username': username,                 'borrow_id': borrow_id,                 'amount': borrow['fine_amount'],                 'status': 'Unpaid',                 'date_issued': return_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')             }             fines[new_fine_id] = fine_record             save_fines(fines)      save_borrowings(borrowings)     save_books(books)      flash('Book returned successfully.', 'success')     return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))  # 11. Cancel Return Action @app.route('/return/cancel/<int:borrow_id>', methods=['POST']) def cancel_return(borrow_id):     return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings'))  # 12. My Reservations Page @app.route('/my-reservations') def my_reservations():     reservations = load_reservations()     books = load_books()     username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      user_reservations = [r for r in reservations.values() if r['username'] == username and r['status'] == 'Active']      res_display = []     for r in user_reservations:         res_display.append({             'reservation_id': r['reservation_id'],             'book_title': books[r['book_id']]['title'] if r['book_id'] in books else 'Unknown',             'reservation_date': r['reservation_date'],             'status': r['status']         })      return render_template('my_reservations.html', reservations=res_display)  # 13. Cancel Reservation Action @app.route('/reservation/cancel/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['POST']) def cancel_reservation(reservation_id):     reservations = load_reservations()     reservation = reservations.get(reservation_id)     if not reservation:         flash('Reservation not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_reservations'))      if reservation['status'] != 'Active':         flash('Reservation is not active.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_reservations'))      reservation['status'] = 'Cancelled'     save_reservations(reservations)      flash('Reservation cancelled successfully.', 'success')     return redirect(url_for('my_reservations'))  # 14. My Reviews page @app.route('/my-reviews') def my_reviews():     reviews = load_reviews()     books = load_books()     username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      user_reviews = [r for r in reviews.values() if r['username'] == username]      reviews_display = []     for r in user_reviews:         reviews_display.append({             'review_id': r['review_id'],             'book_title': books[r['book_id']]['title'] if r['book_id'] in books else 'Unknown',             'rating': r['rating'],             'review_text': r['review_text']         })      return render_template('my_reviews.html', reviews=reviews_display)  # 15. Write Review page (GET and POST) @app.route('/review/write/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def write_review(book_id):     books = load_books()     book = books.get(book_id)     if not book:         flash('Book not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('book_catalog'))      reviews = load_reviews()     username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      # Check for existing review by user for this book     existing_review = None     for review in reviews.values():         if review['username'] == username and review['book_id'] == book_id:             existing_review = review             break      if request.method == 'GET':         return render_template('write_review.html', book=book, existing_review=existing_review)      if request.method == 'POST':         rating = int(request.form.get('rating', '0'))         review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()         if rating < 1 or rating > 5:             flash('Rating must be between 1 and 5.', 'error')             return redirect(url_for('write_review', book_id=book_id))         if not review_text:             flash('Review text cannot be empty.', 'error')             return redirect(url_for('write_review', book_id=book_id))          review_date = datetime.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')          if existing_review:             # Update existing review             existing_review['rating'] = rating             existing_review['review_text'] = review_text             existing_review['review_date'] = review_date         else:             # Add new review             new_review_id = max(reviews.keys(), default=0) + 1             new_review = {                 'review_id': new_review_id,                 'username': username,                 'book_id': book_id,                 'rating': rating,                 'review_text': review_text,                 'review_date': review_date             }             reviews[new_review_id] = new_review          # Save reviews         save_reviews(reviews)          # Update avg_rating in book         book_reviews = [r for r in reviews.values() if r['book_id'] == book_id]         if book_reviews:             avg_rating = sum(r['rating'] for r in book_reviews) / len(book_reviews)             book['avg_rating'] = round(avg_rating, 1)         else:             book['avg_rating'] = 0.0         save_books(books)          flash('Review submitted successfully.', 'success')         return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))  # 16. Edit Review Action (GET and POST) @app.route('/review/edit/<int:review_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def edit_review(review_id):     reviews = load_reviews()     review = reviews.get(review_id)     if not review:         flash('Review not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))      books = load_books()     book = books.get(review['book_id'])     if not book:         flash('Book for review not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))      username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME     if review['username'] != username:         flash('You can only edit your own reviews.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))      if request.method == 'GET':         return render_template('write_review.html', existing_review=review, book=book)      if request.method == 'POST':         rating = int(request.form.get('rating', '0'))         review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()          if rating < 1 or rating > 5:             flash('Rating must be between 1 and 5.', 'error')             return redirect(url_for('edit_review', review_id=review_id))         if not review_text:             flash('Review text cannot be empty.', 'error')             return redirect(url_for('edit_review', review_id=review_id))          review['rating'] = rating         review['review_text'] = review_text         review['review_date'] = datetime.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')          save_reviews(reviews)          # Update avg_rating in book         book_reviews = [r for r in reviews.values() if r['book_id'] == book['book_id']]         if book_reviews:             avg_rating = sum(r['rating'] for r in book_reviews) / len(book_reviews)             book['avg_rating'] = round(avg_rating, 1)         else:             book['avg_rating'] = 0.0         save_books(books)          flash('Review edited successfully.', 'success')         return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))  # 17. Delete Review Action (POST) @app.route('/review/delete/<int:review_id>', methods=['POST']) def delete_review(review_id):     reviews = load_reviews()     review = reviews.get(review_id)     if not review:         flash('Review not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))      username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME     if review['username'] != username:         flash('You can only delete your own reviews.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))      book_id = review['book_id']     del reviews[review_id]     save_reviews(reviews)      # Update avg_rating in book     books = load_books()     book = books.get(book_id)     if book:         book_reviews = [r for r in reviews.values() if r['book_id'] == book_id]         if book_reviews:             avg_rating = sum(r['rating'] for r in book_reviews) / len(book_reviews)             book['avg_rating'] = round(avg_rating, 1)         else:             book['avg_rating'] = 0.0         save_books(books)      flash('Review deleted successfully.', 'success')     return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))  # 18. User Profile Page (GET and POST) @app.route('/profile', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def user_profile():     users = load_users()     username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      if username not in users:         flash('User profile not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))      user = users[username]     borrowings = load_borrowings()     books = load_books()      if request.method == 'GET':         # Prepare borrow history         borrow_history = []         for b in borrowings.values():             if b['username'] == username:                 book_title = books[b['book_id']]['title'] if b['book_id'] in books else 'Unknown'                 borrow_history.append({                     'book_title': book_title,                     'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],                     'return_date': b['return_date'] if b['return_date'] else ''                 })         return render_template('profile.html', user=user, borrow_history=borrow_history)      if request.method == 'POST':         # Process profile update         email = request.form.get('email', '').strip()         phone = request.form.get('phone', '').strip()         address = request.form.get('address', '').strip()          if not email or not phone or not address:             flash('All fields are required.', 'error')             return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))          user['email'] = email         user['phone'] = phone         user['address'] = address          users[username] = user         save_users(users)          flash('Profile updated successfully.', 'success')         return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))  # 19. Payment Confirmation page (GET and POST) @app.route('/payment/<int:fine_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST']) def payment_confirmation(fine_id):     fines = load_fines()     fine = fines.get(fine_id)     if not fine:         flash('Fine record not found.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))      username = LOGGED_IN_USERNAME      if fine['username'] != username:         flash('You can only pay your own fines.', 'error')         return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))      if request.method == 'GET':         return render_template('payment_confirmation.html', fine=fine)      if request.method == 'POST':         # Process payment         if fine['status'] == 'Paid':             flash('Fine is already paid.', 'info')             return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))          fine['status'] = 'Paid'         fines[fine_id] = fine         save_fines(fines)          flash('Payment processed successfully.', 'success')         return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))   if __name__ == '__main__':     app.run(debug=True)
